# Welcome to the Beer Ratings Directory

## How to Use
1. Use the search box to filter beers by name, brewery, or style.
2. Click on any beer name to view detailed ratings and notes.

<script>
  function filterBeers() {
    const searchInput = document.getElementById("searchBox").value.toLowerCase();
    const tableRows = document.getElementById("beerTable").getElementsByTagName("tr");

    for (let i = 1; i < tableRows.length; i++) {
      const cells = tableRows[i].getElementsByTagName("td");
      let rowContainsSearch = false;

      for (let j = 0; j < cells.length; j++) {
        if (cells[j].innerText.toLowerCase().includes(searchInput)) {
          rowContainsSearch = true;
          break;
        }
      }

      tableRows[i].style.display = rowContainsSearch ? "" : "none";
    }
  }
</script>
